# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
a sequence where each element depend on the previous one ^2QqBkJPU

a sequence where each term is the previous with a constant added or an initial term added to a contant n times ^SLNHrn2M

the constant you add to each term of an arithmetic sequence, just subtract a term from the next ^57iPcAR3

the angle measured clockwise from the x axise the point makes on the 
complex plane ^w7anJMtY

the polar form is expressed as r(cos+isin) where r is the modulus of the number and the angle is the
argument of the number ^ggbcasDn

write the number in polar form
set it equal to r(cos + isin)ˆn
compare the moduluses
set the angles as pi+m=alph n
find the alph
find the angle by replacing m with 1,2..n
assemble the pieces ^dUuatADq

the angles should be stated as nt=a+2mpi
state in t (a is the angle of the initial number)
find t with 1,2..n ^eqNpHr7M
